    name = GetCountryBG

        trigger = {
            tag = SOV
        }

    }

        trigger = {
            tag = USA
        } 
        localization_key = "GFX_agency_logo_usa_bg"
    }

        trigger = {
            NOT = { tag = SOV }
            NOT = { tag = USA }
        }
        localization_key = "GFX_agency_logo_usa_bg"
    }
}
